### Round 7: Canadian Grand Prix
*Date: 2014-06-08*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 14: Singapore Grand Prix
*Date: 2014-09-21*

#### Qualifying Results
